## 2. This AWOL Vision UST Projector Earned Best of CES for a Reason

- **频道：** AVS Forum
- **观看数：** 126,900
- **点赞数：** 221
- **评论数：** 84
- **时长：** 6:22
- **发布日期：** 2026-01-09T00:01:18Z
- **链接：** https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=suV8pIgYWGw
- **来源：** search
- **有字幕：** 否
- **语言：** en
- **缩略图：** https://i.ytimg.com/vi/suV8pIgYWGw/hqdefault.jpg
- **标签：** awol vision, awol, projector, ultra short throw projector, ust, ces, ces 2026, ces coverage, awol projector, awol ultra short throw, awol ust, awol aetherion, tv replacement, 4k projector, ces 2026 coverage, gaming projector, avsforum, valerion projector, laser dimming
- **简介：**

  > We stopped by the AWOL Vision booth at CES to check out the company’s newly announced Aetherion Series ultra short throw projectors, including the Aetherion Pro and Aetherion Max.
  > 
  > Both models are designed to deliver a full 4K image at screen sizes up to 200 inches, and AWOL is clearly pushing image quality and optical performance with this new lineup. A motorized dust-seal lens cover is also included to help protect the optical system over time.
  > 
  > Native contrast is rated at 6,000:1, with enhanced black levels reaching up to 60,000:1 using a multi-stage iris system. Brightness is rated at 3,300 ISO lumens for the Aetherion Max and 2,600 ISO lumens for the Aetherion Pro. AWOL also includes anti-RBE technology, claiming a 99.99% reduction in rainbow artifacts, and based on what we saw, it appears to be very effective.
  > 
  > The Aetherion Max was shown on a 200-inch screen right on the show floor, and even in that environment it was plenty bright for watching live sports and looked impressively sharp. Image quality stood out enough that the projector earned an AVSForum Best of CES 2026 award.
  > 
  > Pricing is set at $4,499 for the Aetherion Max and $3,499 for the Aetherion Pro, with availability expected in March 2026.
  > 
  > Be sure to check out our other CES coverage videos for more booth tours, hands-on impressions, and first looks at the latest home theater and AV gear from the show.

## 4. CES 2026: AWOL Vision Unveils Aetherion UST Projector

- **频道：** ProjectorCentral
- **观看数：** 13,215
- **点赞数：** 41
- **评论数：** 3
- **时长：** 5:41
- **发布日期：** 2026-01-20T21:24:10Z
- **链接：** https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=KyI7cZ_0AgI
- **来源：** search
- **有字幕：** 否
- **语言：** en-US
- **缩略图：** https://i.ytimg.com/vi/KyI7cZ_0AgI/hqdefault.jpg
- **简介：**

  > During CES 2026 in Las Vegas on January 6, AWOL Vision, the sister brand of Valerion, unveiled their new ultra short-throw (UST) projector, called Aetherion, which promises 200-inch edge-to-edge sharpness powered by PixelLock technology for precise pixel alignment. 
  > 
  > According to the company, its Aetherion UST model will also exhibit improved dark scene performance with a 6,000:1 native contrast ratio and the brand’s EBL algorithm (60,000:1 viewing contrast) as well as comfortable “omni-format viewing” with anti-RBE (rainbow effect) technology (reducing 99.9% of rainbow artifacts) and TVU-certified blue-light reduction in both 2D and 3D.
  > 
  > Additionally, this new model promises zero-judder, zero-lag gaming enabled by AMD FreeSync Premium, 1ms-class latency, Dolby Vision Gaming, and ALLM. Those are big claims, which Projector Central will test out in our review during Q1 of 2026.

## 16. AWOL Vision &amp; Valerion CES 2026 Booth | Aetherion Laser TV &amp; VisionMaster Max Anamorphic Lens

- **频道：** Projector Reviews
- **观看数：** 16,795
- **点赞数：** 208
- **评论数：** 44
- **时长：** 15:45
- **发布日期：** 2026-01-15T15:14:15Z
- **链接：** https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rR9euQb99G8
- **来源：** search
- **有字幕：** 否
- **语言：** en-US
- **缩略图：** https://i.ytimg.com/vi/rR9euQb99G8/hqdefault.jpg
- **简介：**

  > At CES 2026, Phil Jones visits the shared AWOL Vision and Valerion booth to discuss the new products introduced at the show.
  > 
  > The first half of the video focuses on Valerion, beginning with the transition from the award-winning VisionMaster Pro 2 to the newly shipping VisionMaster Max. Designed as a dedicated home theater projector, the VisionMaster Max adds lens shift, improved black levels, and greater installation flexibility. A key highlight is its interchangeable lens system, which includes standard-throw and long-throw options, allowing the projector to adapt to a wide range of room sizes and layouts.
  > 
  > Valerion also introduces anamorphic lens support, including a custom-designed lens created by a home theater enthusiast with professional optics expertise. When paired with Valerion’s built-in stretch and scope modes, the anamorphic lens allows users to fully utilize the projector’s resolution and light output for CinemaScope content, delivering up to a 30 percent brightness gain while eliminating letterbox bars. Importantly, these features are built directly into the projector, removing the need for expensive external video processors.
  > 
  > The conversation then shifts to AWOL Vision, where Phil revisits the company’s popular first-generation LTV ultra short-throw projectors before diving into the all-new Aetherion series. Available in both Pro and Max versions, the Aetherion represents a true generational upgrade rather than an incremental refresh. AWOL Vision redesigned the optical system to improve edge-to-edge clarity on screens up to 150 and even 200 inches, while also reducing throw distance for easier placement closer to the wall.
  > 
  > The Aetherion models deliver approximately 3,300 lumens of brightness, significantly improved black levels, native contrast ratios up to 6,000:1, and advanced HDR support including Dolby Vision, HDR10+, and Dolby Vision gaming.
  > 
  > Gaming performance is another major highlight, with the Aetherion series leveraging the latest Texas Instruments DLP chipset to achieve ultra-low input lag, including 1080p at 240 frames per second with latency approaching one millisecond, along with variable refresh rate support. 
  > 
  > Additional improvements include enhanced dynamic laser dimming, multi-step iris control, and new anti-rainbow-effect processing.
  > 
  > We also examine AWOL Vision’s broader system solutions, including new Vanish Laser TV systems for the living room, backyard, and outdoor applications. These all-in-one solutions combine a projector, a screen, and weather-resistant enclosures to make large-format projection practical for both permanent and portable installations.
  > 
  > 00:00 – Introduction
  > 00:24 – Valerion VisionMaster Max Overview
  > 01:18 – Interchangeable Lens System Explained
  > 03:00 – Enthusiast-Designed Anamorphic Lens for the VisionMaster Max
  > 04:22 – How Anamorphic Projection Works09:03 – Introducing the Aetherion Pro and Max
  > 13:12 – Vanish Laser TV Systems
  > 15:05 – Kickstarter and Availability Timeline

## 21. Awol Vision Aetherion Max &amp; Pro Revealed | 4K Triple-Laser UST Projectors Explained

  > 
  > Awol Vision highlights its PixelLock™ technology, which is designed to reduce pixel drift and color fringing on ultra-short-throw projectors.
  > Actual performance may vary depending on screen quality, room conditions, and final retail units.
  > 
  > Key specifications include up to 3,300 ISO lumens (Aetherion Max), a claimed 6,000:1 native contrast ratio, and support for Dolby Vision, HDR10+, IMAX Enhanced, and Filmmaker Mode.

## 32. AWOL Vision LTV 3500 review - The brightest 4K Tri Chroma UST laser projector

- **频道：** Nexi Tech
- **观看数：** 180,682

- **简介：**

  > Hi guys! Check out the review of the brightest and the most impressive Tri-Chroma 4K ultra short throw laser projector that I got my hands on. The AWOL Vision LTV-3500 is very powerful 4K UST laser projector that uses three lasers to create image and it has no color wheel.  With the brightness of 3500 lumens and amazing color accuracy out from the box this UST laser projector offers fantastic image quality even with room lights turned on. With the 4K resolution, 3000:1 contrast, screen size up to 150 inches, HDR 10 plus, color gamut 107% REC 2020, 3D support, Low input lag for gaming, Dolby Atmos sound and more the AWOL Vision LTV-3500 is amazing ultra short throw triple laser projector that delivers stunning image quality! Also this projector comes with FIRE TV 4K Max out from the box and the support for Dolby Vision are coming soon. Links are down below.
